Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: cherry\\ \tt RIGHT: jacket\\ \tt TOP: pens\\ \tt BOTTOM: ruler\\ \tt CENTER: toner\\ \tt NORTHWEST: eraser\\ \tt NORTHEAST: pants\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: violet\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: lyre\\ \tt HERE: rake\\ \tt THERE: camellia\\ \tt NOWHERE: eye shadow\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: eagle\\ \tt INSIDE: whale\\ \tt OUTSIDE: toolbelt\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }
